\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Fracture field class. It stores the crack phase field, performs basic operations on them. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{FractureField_8h_source_l00056}{56}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{FractureField_8h_source}{Fracture\+Field.\+h}}.
